      <img src="https://cf.eip.telegraph.co.uk/store/img-media/cb385f99-d27d-47f5-9182-af0f340f835b/cb385f99-d27d-47f5-9182-af0f340f835b-original.svg" srcset="" width="103" height="103" alt="">

<script defer="">
  window.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", (event) => {
    window.dataLayer.event = ["puffDisplay"];
    const profile = tmg.user.getProfile();
    // const profile = {
    // subscriptionTypeExtension: ["Standard"],
    // };
    // console.error("USER PROFILE", profile);

    const subTypes = profile.subscriptionTypeExtension;
    // console.error("SUB TYPES:", subTypes);

    const bannerTypes = window.subscriberBannerTypes;
    // console.error("BANNER TYPES:", bannerTypes);

    const SELECTED_BANNER = window.subscriberBannerPromote;

    // enums
    const EDITORIAL = "EDITORIAL";
    const PUZZLES = "PUZZLES";
    const WINE = "WINE";

    const FULL_ACCESS = "FULL_ACCESS";
    const EDITORIAL_ACCESS = "EDITORIAL_ACCESS";
    const NO_EDITORIAL_ACCESS = "NO_EDITORIAL_ACCESS";

    // sub types and their access types
    const fullAccessTypes = [
      "All Digital Access",
      "7 Day Print",
      "Saturday Print Classic",
      "Complete 6 Day",
      "All Digital Access plus Weekend Newspaers",
      "2 Day Print Classic",
      "Print Editions",
      "Complete 5 Day",
      "Saturday Print",
      "Print Editions 6 Day",
      "All Digital Access plus Sunday Newspaper",
      "Print Editions 5 Day",
      "Unlimited Web Access plus Sunday Newspaper",
      "Events Standard",
      "Events All Digital Access",
      "Unlimited Web Access plus Saturday Newspaper",
      "Print Editions Weekend",
      "Newspaper+",
    ];
    const editorialAccessTypes = ["Standard", "Digital Light"];
    const noAccessTypes = ["Wine", "Puzzles", "Sport", "World Cup Predictor", "All Digital Access Day Pass"];

    let accessType;

    const container = document.getElementById("subscribe__container");
    const banner = document.querySelector(".subscribe__container");
    const header = document.querySelector(".subscribe__header");
    const anchors = document.querySelectorAll(".subscribe__cta");
    const hero = document.querySelector(".subscribe__hero");

    // console.error("CONTAINER:", container);
    // console.error("BANNER", banner);
    // console.error("HERO", hero);

    const paintTemplate = (bannerData, engage = false) => {
      const { name, bg, mobileICON__url, desktopICON__url, logo, acquisitionHeadline, engageHeadline, acquisitionCTA__text, engageCTA__text, acquisitionBody, engageBody, acquisitionCTA__url, engageCTA__url } = bannerData;

      // console.error(acquisitionCTA__url);

      header.firstElementChild.dataset["type"] = name;
      banner.style["background-color"] = bg;
      header.dataset["text"] = engage ? engageHeadline : acquisitionHeadline;
      header.nextElementSibling.textContent = engage ? engageBody : acquisitionBody;
      anchors.forEach((a) => {
        a.dataset["text"] = engage ? engageCTA__text : acquisitionCTA__text;
        a.href = engage ? engageCTA__url : acquisitionCTA__url;
        a.ariaLabel = engage ? engageCTA__text : acquisitionCTA__text;
      });
      hero.firstElementChild.srcset = desktopICON__url ?? mobileICON__url;
      hero.lastElementChild.src = mobileICON__url;

      // console.error("PAINTED ANCHORS", anchors);
    };

    const paintBanner = (bannerData, engage = false) => {
      // IF USER HAS A SUBSCRIPTION THAT MATCHES SELECTED_BANNER
      // THEN ENGAGE = TRUE

      paintTemplate(bannerData, engage);

      if (!accessType || accessType === NO_EDITORIAL_ACCESS) {
        hero.classList.add("lg-image");
        header.firstElementChild.style["display"] = "none";
        banner.style["opacity"] = 1;
        return;
      }

      // PROMO BANNERS FEATURE A LOGO IN THE HEADING

      hero.classList.add("lg-image");
      header.classList.add("desktop__header");
      header.firstElementChild.src = bannerData["logo"];
      banner.style["opacity"] = 1;

      if (bannerData["name"] === "WINE") {
        anchors.forEach((anchor) => anchor.classList.add("wine"));
      }
    };

    const displayBanner = (accessType) => {
      if (!accessType || accessType === NO_EDITORIAL_ACCESS) {
        // console.error("DISPLAY EDITORIAL BANNER");
        const bannerData = bannerTypes[EDITORIAL];
        paintBanner(bannerData);

        return;
      }

      const shouldEngage = (banner) => {
        return profile.subscriptionTypeExtension?.some((type) => type.toLowerCase() === banner.toLowerCase()) || accessType === FULL_ACCESS;
      };

      // console.error("SHOULD ENGAGE?", shouldEngage(SELECTED_BANNER));

      let engage = shouldEngage(SELECTED_BANNER);
      // console.error("ENGAGE:", engage);

      if (accessType === FULL_ACCESS) {
        // console.error("full access, display wine banner");
        const bannerData = bannerTypes[WINE];
        paintBanner(bannerData, engage);
        return;
      }

      //if subbed to DIGITAL + PUZZLES
      // then show PUZZLES engage
      if ((accessType = EDITORIAL_ACCESS && subTypes.some((type) => type.toLowerCase().includes(PUZZLES.toLowerCase())))) {
        const bannerData = bannerTypes[PUZZLES];
        paintBanner(bannerData, true);

        return;
      }

      if (subTypes.some((type) => type.toLowerCase().includes(SELECTED_BANNER.toLowerCase()))) {
        //if subbed to promo banner already
        // console.error("DISPLAYING ALTERNATE BANNER SINCE THEY ARE ALREADY SUBBED TO SELECTED BANNER TYPE");
        const banners = Object.keys(bannerTypes)
          .slice(1) // REMOVE 'EDITORIAL' BANNER
          .filter((type) => !type.toLowerCase().includes(SELECTED_BANNER.toLowerCase()));

        const bannerToShow = banners[Math.floor(Math.random() * banners.length)];

        const bannerData = bannerTypes[bannerToShow];
        // console.error("BANNER TO SHOW", bannerToShow);
        // console.error("BANNER DATA:", bannerData);

        engage = shouldEngage(bannerToShow);
        paintBanner(bannerData, engage);
        return;
      }

      // console.error(`DISPLAYING ${SELECTED_BANNER} BANNER`);
      const bannerData = bannerTypes[SELECTED_BANNER];
      // console.error("BANNER DATA", bannerData);

      paintBanner(bannerData, engage);
      return;
    };

    // IF NO PROFILE
    if (!profile || profile.subscriber === "false" || !profile.subscriptionTypeExtension) {
      // console.error("NO PROFILE, PAINTING EDITORIAL...", profile);
      displayBanner(NO_EDITORIAL_ACCESS);
      return;
    }

    // DETERMINE ACCESS TYPE
    switch (true) {
      // IF SUB TYPES MATCH FULL ACCESS TYPES
      case fullAccessTypes.some((str) => subTypes.some((type) => type.toLowerCase().includes(str.toLowerCase()))): {
        accessType = FULL_ACCESS;
        break;
      }
      // IF SUB TYPES MATCH EDITORIAL ACCESS TYPES
      case editorialAccessTypes.some((str) => subTypes.some((type) => type.toLowerCase().includes(str.toLowerCase()))): {
        accessType = EDITORIAL_ACCESS;
        break;
      }
      // IF SUB TYPES MATCH NO EDITORIAL ACCESS TYPES
      case noAccessTypes.some((str) => subTypes.some((type) => type.toLowerCase().includes(str.toLowerCase()))): {
        accessType = NO_EDITORIAL_ACCESS;
        break;
      }
      // NO MATCHING SUB TYPES
      default: {
        // console.error("NO MATCHING SUB TYPES ");
        accessType = NO_EDITORIAL_ACCESS;
        displayBanner(NO_EDITORIAL_ACCESS);
        return;
      }
    }
    console.error("ACCESS TYPE:", accessType);

    displayBanner(accessType);
  });
</script>











		</div>

			<div class="card-image u-order-start">
				

	
		
		

		
		

		
		

		
		

		
		

	
		
		

		
		
			
		

		
		

		
		

		
		

		

		
			
		

	
	
		<div class="grid-col grid-col-4 package__image package__image--large">
			<a rel=" " href="/news/2023/02/12/caring-friends-tribute-surrey-dog-walker-natasha-johnston-pictures/">
				<figure class="package__figure" data-test="package-figure">
